H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc <- readRDS("data/Data_Sets/H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc.RDS")
Enrich_Go_sets <- function(gene_sets, v) {

  library(clusterProfiler)
  library(org.Hs.eg.db)
  library(dplyr)

  # -----------------------------
  # Universe (FIXED)
  # -----------------------------
  background_genes <- rownames(v$E) %>%
    sub("\\..*", "", .)

  # -----------------------------
  # GO helper
  # -----------------------------
  run_go <- function(genes) {

    genes <- unique(sub("\\..*", "", genes))

    if (length(genes) < 10) return(NULL)

    ego <- enrichGO(
      gene          = genes,
      universe      = background_genes,
      OrgDb         = org.Hs.eg.db,
      keyType       = "ENSEMBL",
      ont           = "BP",
      readable      = TRUE
    )

    if (is.null(ego)) return(NULL)

    as.data.frame(ego)
  }

  # -----------------------------
  # Run for each gene set
  # -----------------------------
  results <- lapply(gene_sets, function(df) {
    if (is.null(df) || nrow(df) == 0) return(NULL)
    run_go(df$Gene)
  })

  return(results)
}

 metadata$Timepoint <- factor(
   metadata$Timepoint,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

design_int <- model.matrix(~ Species * Timepoint,
                           data =  metadata)

colnames(design_int)

species_levels <- unique(metadata$Species)
day_levels <- unique(metadata$Timepoint)

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,
        main = paste(sp, day),
        legend = FALSE,
        axes = FALSE
      )

      axis(1)
      axis(2)
      mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

      legend(
        "right",
        legend = metadata$Individual[idx],
        col = cols,
        lty = 1,
        cex = 0.7
      )
    }
  }
}

dge <- readRDS("data/DGE/dge_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
design_int <- readRDS("data/DGE/design_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
v1 <- readRDS("data/DGE/v1_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
fit <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

contrast_matrix <- makeContrasts(

  # Species differences
  HvC_Day0  = SpeciesH,
  HvC_Day2  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  HvC_Day5  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  HvC_Day15 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  HvC_Day30 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30,
  
  #Trajectory differences
  H_Day02 = TimepointDay2 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day25 = TimepointDay5 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day515 = TimepointDay15 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  H_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  C_Day02 = TimepointDay2,
  C_Day25 = TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2,
  C_Day515 = TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5,
  C_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15,
  
  # True interaction tests trajectory
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  
  levels = design_int
)

fit2 <- contrasts.fit(fit, contrast_matrix)
fit2 <- eBayes(fit2)

plotSA(fit2, main = "H3K27ac Model")

results_summary <- decideTests(fit2,
                               adjust.method = "BH",
                               p.value = 0.05)
summary(results_summary)

# saveRDS(fit2, "data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

#Create Human TopTable. using listapply, then you can pull specific comp using the $
TopTables_H3K27ac_names <- colnames(fit2$coefficients) 

TopTable_H3K27ac_All <- do.call(
  rbind,
  lapply(TopTables_H3K27ac_names,function(ct) {
    
    tt <- topTable(
      fit2,
      coef = ct,
      number = Inf,
      sort.by = "p"
    )
    
    #add identifiers
    tt$Gene <- rownames(tt)
    tt$Comparisons <- ct
    
    tt
  })
)

ComparisonNames <- unique(TopTable_H3K27ac_All$Comparisons)

saveRDS(TopTable_H3K27ac_All, "data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
saveRDS(ComparisonNames, "data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(stringr)
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

hvcdays <- names(H3K27ac_sets)[str_detect(names(H3K27ac_sets), "^HvC_")]

prop_df <- map_dfr(hvcdays, function(traj) {
  
  x <- H3K27ac_sets[[traj]]
  
  tibble(
    trajectory = traj,
    DEG = length(x$DEGs$Gene),
    NonDEG = length(x$NonDEGs$Gene)
  )
})
library(tidyr)

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(cols = c(DEG, NonDEG),
               names_to = "type",
               values_to = "count") %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()
prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("HvC_Day0", "HvC_Day2", "HvC_Day5", "HvC_Day15", "HvC_Day30"),
  labels = c("0", "2", "5", "15", "30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = "",
    title = "HvC comparisons: DEG vs NonDEG composition"
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

timepoints <- c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Time = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes_list <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

ggVennDiagram(genes_list, label = "count") +
  scale_fill_gradient(low = "white", high = "steelblue") +
  theme(
    panel.grid = element_blank(),
    panel.background = element_blank(),
    axis.text = element_text(size = 10),
    plot.title = element_text(face = "bold")
  )

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

days <- names(genes)

shared_all <- Reduce(intersect, genes)

get_fate <- function(day) {

  g <- genes[[day]]

  specific <- setdiff(g, unlist(genes[names(genes) != day]))

  shared_all_day <- intersect(g, shared_all)

  shared_partial <- setdiff(
    setdiff(g, specific),
    shared_all_day
  )

  data.frame(
    Day = day,
    Specific = length(specific),
    Shared_partial = length(shared_partial),
    Shared_all = length(shared_all_day)
  )
}

plot_df <- do.call(rbind, lapply(names(genes), get_fate))

library(tidyr)

plot_long <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  )

plot_long$Day <- factor(
  plot_long$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long, aes(x = Day, y = Count, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
    scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Number of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)

plot_long_prop <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(Day) %>%
  mutate(
    Prop = Count / sum(Count)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

plot_long_prop$Day <- factor(
  plot_long_prop$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long_prop, aes(x = Day, y = Prop, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
  
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Proportion of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development (normalized)"
  )

    "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",

traj_info <- list(
  Traj02_genes = list(coef = "H_Day02", comp = "Day02"),
  Traj25_genes = list(coef = "H_Day25", comp = "Day25"),
  Traj515_genes = list(coef ="H_Day515", comp = "Day515"),
 Traj1530_genes = list(coef = "H_Day1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

H_comp <- "H_Day02"
C_comp <- "C_Day02"

df_wide <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(H_comp, C_comp)) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  group_by(Gene, Comparisons) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = Comparisons, values_from = logFC) %>%
  filter(!is.na(.data[[H_comp]]), !is.na(.data[[C_comp]]))

# head(df_wide)
# nrow(df_wide)

fit <- lm(df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])
summary(fit)

Call:
lm(formula = df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])

Residuals:
    Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max 
-3.6447 -0.4216 -0.0055  0.4165  3.6409 

Coefficients:
                   Estimate Std. Error t value Pr(>|t|)    
(Intercept)       -0.058040   0.001110  -52.31   <2e-16 ***
df_wide[[H_comp]]  0.221043   0.001535  144.04   <2e-16 ***
---
Signif. codes:  0 '***' 0.001 '**' 0.01 '*' 0.05 '.' 0.1 ' ' 1

Residual standard error: 0.6916 on 389828 degrees of freedom
Multiple R-squared:  0.05053,   Adjusted R-squared:  0.05053 
F-statistic: 2.075e+04 on 1 and 389828 DF,  p-value: < 2.2e-16
r2 <- summary(fit)$r.squared
pval <- summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]

# r2
# pval

format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
[1] "0e+00"
library(ggplot2)

x_pos <- max(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.95      # right side
x_neg <- min(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.5      # left side

y_pos <- max(df_wide[[C_comp]]) * 0.95

# Optional: make axes symmetric around 0 for a nicer visual
x_limits <- c(-7, 7)
y_limits <- c(-7, 7)


genes_of_interest_human <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$H_Day02$DEGs$Gene)
genes_of_interest_chimp <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$C_Day02$DEGs$Gene)

df_wide$highlight <- dplyr::case_when(
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human &
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Both",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human ~ "T-DEG Human Only",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Chimp Only",

  TRUE ~ "Other"
)

# Plot
ggplot(df_wide, aes(x = .data[[H_comp]], y = .data[[C_comp]], color = highlight)) +
  geom_point(size = 3, alpha = 0.8) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("T-DEG Human Only" = "red", "T-DEG Chimp Only" = "blue", "T-DEG Both" = "purple", "Other" = "grey70")) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, linetype = "dashed", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  annotate(
    "text",
    x = min(df_wide[[H_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    y = max(df_wide[[C_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    label = paste0(
      "R² = ", round(r2, 3),
      "\np = ", format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
    ),
    hjust = 0,
    vjust = 1
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(xlim = x_limits, ylim = y_limits) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = H_comp,
    y = C_comp,
    title = paste0(H_comp, " vs ", C_comp),
    color = "Gene Set"
  )

library(tidyr)
library(stringr)

df_all <- TopTable %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  
  mutate(
    species = ifelse(str_starts(Comparisons, "H_"), "H", "C"),
    trajectory = str_remove(Comparisons, "^[HC]_")
  ) %>%
  
  group_by(Gene, species, trajectory) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  
  pivot_wider(names_from = species, values_from = logFC) %>%
  
  filter(!is.na(H), !is.na(C))

library(ggplot2)

df_all$trajectory <- df_all$trajectory <- factor(
  df_all$trajectory,
  levels = c("Day02", "Day25", "Day515","Day1530")
)

ggplot(df_all, aes(x = H, y = C, color = trajectory)) +
  geom_point(alpha = 0.7) +
  
  # one regression line per trajectory (same color as points)
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, fullrange = TRUE)+
  
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Human logFC",
    y = "Chimp logFC",
    color = "Trajectory",
    title = "All Trajectories Combined"
  )

df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  do({
    fit <- lm(C ~ H, data = .)
    data.frame(
      r2 = summary(fit)$r.squared,
      p = summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]
    )
  })
dge <- readRDS("data/DGE/dge_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
design_int <- readRDS("data/DGE/design_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
v1 <- readRDS("data/DGE/v1_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
fit <-readRDS("data/DGE/fit_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <-readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
direction_results <- readRDS("data/DGE/Trajectory_Directions_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
  
traj_levels <- c("H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
                 "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530")

df <- TopTable %>%
  dplyr::filter(Comparisons %in% traj_levels)

df <- df %>%
  dplyr::mutate(
    Species = ifelse(grepl("^H", Comparisons), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = sub(".*_(Day[0-9]+)", "\\1", Comparisons),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

df_deg <- df %>%
  dplyr::filter(DEG)

library(dplyr)

df_deg2 <- df_deg %>%
  group_by(Gene, Stage, Species) %>%
  summarise(.groups = "drop")

df_overlap <- df_deg2 %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = Gene,
    values_fn = length,
    values_fill = 0
  )

df_flags <- df_deg2 %>%
  mutate(flag = TRUE) %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = flag,
    values_fill = FALSE
  ) %>%
  dplyr::mutate(
    category = case_when(
      Human & Chimp ~ "Shared",
      Human ~ "Human only",
      Chimp ~ "Chimp only"
    )
  )

plot_df <- df_flags %>%
  group_by(Stage, category) %>%
  summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
  group_by(Stage) %>%
  mutate(prop = n / sum(n))

plot_df$Stage <- factor(
  plot_df$Stage,
  levels = c("Day02", "Day25", "Day515", "Day1530")
)

library(ggpattern)

ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Stage, y = n, fill = category)) +

  geom_col_pattern(
    aes(pattern = category),
    colour = "black",
    pattern_colour = "black",
    pattern_fill = "white",
    pattern_density = 0.4,
    pattern_spacing = 0.02
  ) +

  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "grey70",
    "Human only" = "black",
    "Chimp only" = "white"
  )) +

  scale_pattern_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "stripe",
    "Human only" = "none",
    "Chimp only" = "none"
  )) +

  theme_minimal(base_size = 14) +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental Stage",
    y = "Count",
    fill = "",
    pattern = ""
  )

ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Stage, y = prop, fill = category)) +

  geom_col_pattern(
    aes(pattern = category),
    colour = "black",
    pattern_colour = "black",
    pattern_fill = "white",
    pattern_density = 0.4,
    pattern_spacing = 0.02
  ) +

  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "grey70",
    "Human only" = "black",
    "Chimp only" = "white"
  )) +

  scale_pattern_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "stripe",
    "Human only" = "none",
    "Chimp only" = "none"
  )) +

  theme_minimal(base_size = 14) +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental Stage",
    y = "Proportion of DERs",
    fill = "",
    pattern = ""
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")

traj_info <- list(
  InterTraj02 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02", comp = "Day02"),
  InterTraj25 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25", comp = "Day25"),
  InterTraj515 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515", comp = "Day515"),
  InterTraj1530 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

cluster_lists <- list(
  InterTraj02  = Inter_02_genes,
  InterTraj25  = Inter_25_genes,
  InterTraj515 = Inter_515_genes,
  InterTraj1530 = Inter_1530_genes
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

###Reproducible3 ####Stats

library(edgeR)

counts_table <- readRDS("data/Data_Sets/H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc.RDS")
metadata <- readRDS("data/Data_Sets/H3K27ac_Metadata.RDS")

counts <- counts_table %>%
  dplyr::select(!matches("Day4")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("C3647_Day30")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("C40210_Day15")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("C3649_Day4")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("C3649_Day0")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("C40280_Day2")) %>%
  dplyr::select(-contains("H24280_Day2"))

metadata <- metadata %>%
  filter(Timepoint != "Day4") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "C3647_Day30") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "C40210_Day15") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "C3649_Day4") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "H24280_Day2") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "C3649_Day0") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "C40280_Day2") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "H20682R_Day0") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "H20682R_Day2") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "H20682R_Day5") %>%
  filter(SampleName != "H20682R_Day30")

counts_norep <- counts %>%
  dplyr::select(-(contains("R")))


#create DGEList object
dge <- DGEList(counts = counts_norep)
dge$samples$group <- factor(metadata$Cond)

species_levels <- unique(metadata$Species)
day_levels <- unique(metadata$Timepoint)

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,
        main = paste(sp, day),
        legend = FALSE,
        axes = FALSE
      )

      axis(1)
      axis(2)
      mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

      legend(
        "right",
        legend = metadata$Individual[idx],
        col = cols,
        lty = 1,
        cex = 0.7
      )
    }
  }
}

v1 <- readRDS("data/DGE/v1_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
fit <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

contrast_matrix <- makeContrasts(

  # Species differences
  HvC_Day0  = SpeciesH,
  HvC_Day2  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  HvC_Day5  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  HvC_Day15 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  HvC_Day30 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30,
  
  #Trajectory differences
  H_Day02 = TimepointDay2 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day25 = TimepointDay5 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day515 = TimepointDay15 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  H_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  C_Day02 = TimepointDay2,
  C_Day25 = TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2,
  C_Day515 = TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5,
  C_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15,
  
  # True interaction tests trajectory
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  
  levels = design_int
)

fit2 <- contrasts.fit(fit, contrast_matrix)
fit2 <- eBayes(fit2)

plotSA(fit2, main = "H3K27ac Model")

results_summary <- decideTests(fit2,
                               adjust.method = "BH",
                               p.value = 0.05)
summary(results_summary)

# saveRDS(fit2, "data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

#Create Human TopTable. using listapply, then you can pull specific comp using the $
TopTables_H3K27ac_names <- colnames(fit2$coefficients) 

TopTable_H3K27ac_All <- do.call(
  rbind,
  lapply(TopTables_H3K27ac_names,function(ct) {
    
    tt <- topTable(
      fit2,
      coef = ct,
      number = Inf,
      sort.by = "p"
    )
    
    #add identifiers
    tt$Gene <- rownames(tt)
    tt$Comparisons <- ct
    
    tt
  })
)

ComparisonNames <- unique(TopTable_H3K27ac_All$Comparisons)

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

# Calculate global axis limits
x_limits <- range(TopTable$logFC, na.rm = TRUE)
y_limits <- range(-log10(TopTable$P.Value), na.rm = TRUE)

plot <- list()

for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  data_n <- TopTable %>% 
    dplyr::filter(Comparisons == n)
  
  plot[[n]] <- generate_volcano_plot(data_n, n) +
    ggplot2::xlim(x_limits) +
    ggplot2::ylim(y_limits)
}

# Print plots
for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  print(plot[[n]])
}

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- map(
  ComparisonNames,
  ~ {
    df <- TopTable %>%
      filter(Comparisons == paste0(.x))

    list(
      DEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val < 0.05),
      NonDEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val >= 0.05)
    )
  }
)


names(H3K27ac_sets) <- paste0(ComparisonNames)

saveRDS(H3K27ac_sets, "data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

Species_DEG_info <- list(
  HvC_Day0 = list(coef = "HvC_Day0", comp = "HvC_Day0"),
  HvC_Day2 = list(coef = "HvC_Day2", comp = "HvC_Day2"),
  HvC_Day5 = list(coef ="HvC_Day5", comp = "HvC_Day5"),
 HvC_Day15 = list(coef = "HvC_Day15", comp = "HvC_Day15"),
 HvC_Day30 = list(coef = "HvC_Day30", comp = "HvC_Day30")
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(Species_DEG_info), function(name) {

    info <- Species_DEG_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions_HvC(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2
    )

  }),
  names(Species_DEG_info)
)

saveRDS(direction_results, "data/DGE/Species_Directions_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

  filter(Comparisons %in% c(
    "HvC_Day0","HvC_Day2","HvC_Day5","HvC_Day15",
    "HvC_Day30"
  ))

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(stringr)
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

hvcdays <- names(H3K27ac_sets)[str_detect(names(H3K27ac_sets), "^HvC_")]

prop_df <- map_dfr(hvcdays, function(traj) {
  
  x <- H3K27ac_sets[[traj]]
  
  tibble(
    trajectory = traj,
    DEG = length(x$DEGs$Gene),
    NonDEG = length(x$NonDEGs$Gene)
  )
})
library(tidyr)

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(cols = c(DEG, NonDEG),
               names_to = "type",
               values_to = "count") %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()
prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("HvC_Day0", "HvC_Day2", "HvC_Day5", "HvC_Day15", "HvC_Day30"),
  labels = c("0", "2", "5", "15", "30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = "",
    title = "HvC comparisons: DEG vs NonDEG composition"
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

timepoints <- c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Time = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes_list <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

ggVennDiagram(genes_list, label = "count") +
  scale_fill_gradient(low = "white", high = "steelblue") +
  theme(
    panel.grid = element_blank(),
    panel.background = element_blank(),
    axis.text = element_text(size = 10),
    plot.title = element_text(face = "bold")
  )

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

days <- names(genes)

shared_all <- Reduce(intersect, genes)

get_fate <- function(day) {

  g <- genes[[day]]

  specific <- setdiff(g, unlist(genes[names(genes) != day]))

  shared_all_day <- intersect(g, shared_all)

  shared_partial <- setdiff(
    setdiff(g, specific),
    shared_all_day
  )

  data.frame(
    Day = day,
    Specific = length(specific),
    Shared_partial = length(shared_partial),
    Shared_all = length(shared_all_day)
  )
}

plot_df <- do.call(rbind, lapply(names(genes), get_fate))

library(tidyr)

plot_long <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  )

plot_long$Day <- factor(
  plot_long$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long, aes(x = Day, y = Count, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
    scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Number of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)

plot_long_prop <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(Day) %>%
  mutate(
    Prop = Count / sum(Count)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

plot_long_prop$Day <- factor(
  plot_long_prop$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long_prop, aes(x = Day, y = Prop, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
  
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Proportion of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development (normalized)"
  )

traj_info <- list(
  Traj02_genes = list(coef = "H_Day02", comp = "Day02"),
  Traj25_genes = list(coef = "H_Day25", comp = "Day25"),
  Traj515_genes = list(coef ="H_Day515", comp = "Day515"),
 Traj1530_genes = list(coef = "H_Day1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

H_comp <- "H_Day02"
C_comp <- "C_Day02"

df_wide <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(H_comp, C_comp)) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  group_by(Gene, Comparisons) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = Comparisons, values_from = logFC) %>%
  filter(!is.na(.data[[H_comp]]), !is.na(.data[[C_comp]]))

# head(df_wide)
# nrow(df_wide)

fit <- lm(df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])
summary(fit)

Call:
lm(formula = df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])

Residuals:
    Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max 
-3.5669 -0.3705 -0.0038  0.3676  3.6772 

Coefficients:
                   Estimate Std. Error t value Pr(>|t|)    
(Intercept)       -0.030886   0.001506  -20.51   <2e-16 ***
df_wide[[H_comp]]  0.375343   0.002290  163.90   <2e-16 ***
---
Signif. codes:  0 '***' 0.001 '**' 0.01 '*' 0.05 '.' 0.1 ' ' 1

Residual standard error: 0.6378 on 179848 degrees of freedom
Multiple R-squared:   0.13, Adjusted R-squared:   0.13 
F-statistic: 2.686e+04 on 1 and 179848 DF,  p-value: < 2.2e-16
r2 <- summary(fit)$r.squared
pval <- summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]

# r2
# pval

format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
[1] "0e+00"
library(ggplot2)

x_pos <- max(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.95      # right side
x_neg <- min(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.5      # left side

y_pos <- max(df_wide[[C_comp]]) * 0.95

# Optional: make axes symmetric around 0 for a nicer visual
x_limits <- c(-7, 7)
y_limits <- c(-7, 7)


genes_of_interest_human <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$H_Day02$DEGs$Gene)
genes_of_interest_chimp <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$C_Day02$DEGs$Gene)

df_wide$highlight <- dplyr::case_when(
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human &
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Both",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human ~ "T-DEG Human Only",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Chimp Only",

  TRUE ~ "Other"
)

# Plot
ggplot(df_wide, aes(x = .data[[H_comp]], y = .data[[C_comp]], color = highlight)) +
  geom_point(size = 3, alpha = 0.8) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("T-DEG Human Only" = "red", "T-DEG Chimp Only" = "blue", "T-DEG Both" = "purple", "Other" = "grey70")) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, linetype = "dashed", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  annotate(
    "text",
    x = min(df_wide[[H_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    y = max(df_wide[[C_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    label = paste0(
      "R² = ", round(r2, 3),
      "\np = ", format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
    ),
    hjust = 0,
    vjust = 1
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(xlim = x_limits, ylim = y_limits) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = H_comp,
    y = C_comp,
    title = paste0(H_comp, " vs ", C_comp),
    color = "Gene Set"
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
direction_results <- readRDS("data/DGE/Trajectory_Directions_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible2_fc_No4.RDS")
  
traj_levels <- c("H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
                 "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530")

df <- TopTable %>%
  dplyr::filter(Comparisons %in% traj_levels)

df <- df %>%
  dplyr::mutate(
    Species = ifelse(grepl("^H", Comparisons), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = sub(".*_(Day[0-9]+)", "\\1", Comparisons),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

df_deg <- df %>%
  dplyr::filter(DEG)

library(dplyr)

df_deg2 <- df_deg %>%
  group_by(Gene, Stage, Species) %>%
  summarise(.groups = "drop")

df_overlap <- df_deg2 %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = Gene,
    values_fn = length,
    values_fill = 0
  )

df_flags <- df_deg2 %>%
  mutate(flag = TRUE) %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = flag,
    values_fill = FALSE
  ) %>%
  dplyr::mutate(
    category = case_when(
      Human & Chimp ~ "Shared",
      Human ~ "Human only",
      Chimp ~ "Chimp only"
    )
  )

plot_df <- df_flags %>%
  group_by(Stage, category) %>%
  summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
  group_by(Stage) %>%
  mutate(prop = n / sum(n))

plot_df$Stage <- factor(
  plot_df$Stage,
  levels = c("Day02", "Day25", "Day515", "Day1530")
)

library(ggpattern)

ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Stage, y = n, fill = category)) +

  geom_col_pattern(
    aes(pattern = category),
    colour = "black",
    pattern_colour = "black",
    pattern_fill = "white",
    pattern_density = 0.4,
    pattern_spacing = 0.02
  ) +

  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "grey70",
    "Human only" = "black",
    "Chimp only" = "white"
  )) +

  scale_pattern_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "stripe",
    "Human only" = "none",
    "Chimp only" = "none"
  )) +

  theme_minimal(base_size = 14) +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental Stage",
    y = "Count",
    fill = "",
    pattern = ""
  )

ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Stage, y = prop, fill = category)) +

  geom_col_pattern(
    aes(pattern = category),
    colour = "black",
    pattern_colour = "black",
    pattern_fill = "white",
    pattern_density = 0.4,
    pattern_spacing = 0.02
  ) +

  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "grey70",
    "Human only" = "black",
    "Chimp only" = "white"
  )) +

  scale_pattern_manual(values = c(
    "Shared" = "stripe",
    "Human only" = "none",
    "Chimp only" = "none"
  )) +

  theme_minimal(base_size = 14) +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental Stage",
    y = "Proportion of DERs",
    fill = "",
    pattern = ""
  )

ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

TopTable_H3K27ac_Traj <- TopTable %>% 
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(
    "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
    "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
  ))

Inter_02_genes <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02$DEGs$Gene)
Inter_25_genes <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25$DEGs$Gene)
Inter_515_genes <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515$DEGs$Gene)
Inter_1530_genes <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530$DEGs$Gene)

cluster_lists <- list(
  Inter_02_genes  = Inter_02_genes,
  Inter_25_genes  = Inter_25_genes,
  Inter_515_genes  = Inter_515_genes,
  Inter_1530_genes  = Inter_1530_genes
)

cluster_plots <- lapply(names(cluster_lists), function(clust_name) {
  plot_cluster_fc_sig_trajectory_No4(cluster_lists[[clust_name]], clust_name, TopTable_H3K27ac_Traj)
})

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
ComparisonNames <- readRDS("data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

traj_info <- list(
  InterTraj02 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02", comp = "Day02"),
  InterTraj25 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25", comp = "Day25"),
  InterTraj515 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515", comp = "Day515"),
  InterTraj1530 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

cluster_lists <- list(
  InterTraj02  = Inter_02_genes,
  InterTraj25  = Inter_25_genes,
  InterTraj515 = Inter_515_genes,
  InterTraj1530 = Inter_1530_genes
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

saveRDS(direction_results, "data/DGE/Interaction_Directions_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible3_fc_No4.RDS")

metadata$Species <- factor(
  metadata$Species,
  levels = c("C", "H")   # Chimp baseline
)

 metadata$Timepoint <- factor(
   metadata$Timepoint,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

design_int <- model.matrix(~ Species * Timepoint,
                           data =  metadata)

colnames(design_int)
 [1] "(Intercept)"             "SpeciesH"               
 [3] "TimepointDay2"           "TimepointDay5"          
 [5] "TimepointDay15"          "TimepointDay30"         
 [7] "SpeciesH:TimepointDay2"  "SpeciesH:TimepointDay5" 
 [9] "SpeciesH:TimepointDay15" "SpeciesH:TimepointDay30"
colnames(design_int) <- make.names(colnames(design_int))

species_levels <- unique(metadata$Species)
day_levels <- unique(metadata$Timepoint)

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,
        main = paste(sp, day),
        legend = FALSE,
        axes = FALSE
      )

      axis(1)
      axis(2)
      mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

      legend(
        "right",
        legend = metadata$Individual[idx],
        col = cols,
        lty = 1,
        cex = 0.7
      )
    }
  }
}

dge <- readRDS("data/DGE/dge_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")
design_int <- readRDS("data/DGE/design_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")
v1 <- readRDS("data/DGE/v1_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")
fit <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

contrast_matrix <- makeContrasts(

  # Species differences
  HvC_Day0  = SpeciesH,
  HvC_Day2  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  HvC_Day5  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  HvC_Day15 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  HvC_Day30 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30,
  
  #Trajectory differences
  H_Day02 = TimepointDay2 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day25 = TimepointDay5 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day515 = TimepointDay15 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  H_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  C_Day02 = TimepointDay2,
  C_Day25 = TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2,
  C_Day515 = TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5,
  C_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15,
  
  # True interaction tests trajectory
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  
  levels = design_int
)

fit2 <- contrasts.fit(fit, contrast_matrix)
fit2 <- eBayes(fit2)

plotSA(fit2, main = "H3K27ac Model")

results_summary <- decideTests(fit2,
                               adjust.method = "BH",
                               p.value = 0.05)
summary(results_summary)

fit2 <- readRDS("data/DGE/fit2_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

#Create Human TopTable. using listapply, then you can pull specific comp using the $
TopTables_H3K27ac_names <- colnames(fit2$coefficients) 

TopTable_H3K27ac_All <- do.call(
  rbind,
  lapply(TopTables_H3K27ac_names,function(ct) {
    
    tt <- topTable(
      fit2,
      coef = ct,
      number = Inf,
      sort.by = "p"
    )
    
    #add identifiers
    tt$Gene <- rownames(tt)
    tt$Comparisons <- ct
    
    tt
  })
)

ComparisonNames <- unique(TopTable_H3K27ac_All$Comparisons)

saveRDS(TopTable_H3K27ac_All, "data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")
saveRDS(ComparisonNames, "data/DGE/ComparisonNames_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

  }

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(stringr)
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

hvcdays <- names(H3K27ac_sets)[str_detect(names(H3K27ac_sets), "^HvC_")]

prop_df <- map_dfr(hvcdays, function(traj) {
  
  x <- H3K27ac_sets[[traj]]
  
  tibble(
    trajectory = traj,
    DEG = length(x$DEGs$Gene),
    NonDEG = length(x$NonDEGs$Gene)
  )
})
library(tidyr)

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(cols = c(DEG, NonDEG),
               names_to = "type",
               values_to = "count") %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()
prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("HvC_Day0", "HvC_Day2", "HvC_Day5", "HvC_Day15", "HvC_Day30"),
  labels = c("0", "2", "5", "15", "30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = "",
    title = "HvC comparisons: DEG vs NonDEG composition"
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

timepoints <- c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Time = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes_list <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Time == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Time == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

ggVennDiagram(genes_list, label = "count") +
  scale_fill_gradient(low = "white", high = "steelblue") +
  theme(
    panel.grid = element_blank(),
    panel.background = element_blank(),
    axis.text = element_text(size = 10),
    plot.title = element_text(face = "bold")
  )

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

days <- names(genes)

shared_all <- Reduce(intersect, genes)

get_fate <- function(day) {

  g <- genes[[day]]

  specific <- setdiff(g, unlist(genes[names(genes) != day]))

  shared_all_day <- intersect(g, shared_all)

  shared_partial <- setdiff(
    setdiff(g, specific),
    shared_all_day
  )

  data.frame(
    Day = day,
    Specific = length(specific),
    Shared_partial = length(shared_partial),
    Shared_all = length(shared_all_day)
  )
}

plot_df <- do.call(rbind, lapply(names(genes), get_fate))

library(tidyr)

plot_long <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  )

plot_long$Day <- factor(
  plot_long$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long, aes(x = Day, y = Count, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
    scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Number of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)

plot_long_prop <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(Day) %>%
  mutate(
    Prop = Count / sum(Count)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

plot_long_prop$Day <- factor(
  plot_long_prop$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long_prop, aes(x = Day, y = Prop, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
  
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Proportion of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development (normalized)"
  )

TopTable <- readRDS("data/DGE/TopTable_H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")
H3K27ac_sets <- readRDS("data/DGE/H3K27ac_sets__H3K27ac_hg38_Reproducible4_fc_No4.RDS")

H_comp <- "H_Day02"
C_comp <- "C_Day02"

df_wide <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(H_comp, C_comp)) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  group_by(Gene, Comparisons) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = Comparisons, values_from = logFC) %>%
  filter(!is.na(.data[[H_comp]]), !is.na(.data[[C_comp]]))

# head(df_wide)
# nrow(df_wide)

fit <- lm(df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])
summary(fit)

Call:
lm(formula = df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])

Residuals:
    Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max 
-3.2270 -0.3232 -0.0051  0.3180  3.4343 

Coefficients:
                   Estimate Std. Error t value Pr(>|t|)    
(Intercept)       -0.026427   0.001719  -15.37   <2e-16 ***
df_wide[[H_comp]]  0.473514   0.002744  172.57   <2e-16 ***
---
Signif. codes:  0 '***' 0.001 '**' 0.01 '*' 0.05 '.' 0.1 ' ' 1

Residual standard error: 0.5589 on 105833 degrees of freedom
Multiple R-squared:  0.2196,    Adjusted R-squared:  0.2196 
F-statistic: 2.978e+04 on 1 and 105833 DF,  p-value: < 2.2e-16
r2 <- summary(fit)$r.squared
pval <- summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]

# r2
# pval

format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
[1] "0e+00"
library(ggplot2)

x_pos <- max(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.95      # right side
x_neg <- min(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.5      # left side

y_pos <- max(df_wide[[C_comp]]) * 0.95

# Optional: make axes symmetric around 0 for a nicer visual
x_limits <- c(-7, 7)
y_limits <- c(-7, 7)


genes_of_interest_human <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$H_Day02$DEGs$Gene)
genes_of_interest_chimp <- unique(H3K27ac_sets$C_Day02$DEGs$Gene)

df_wide$highlight <- dplyr::case_when(
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human &
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Both",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human ~ "T-DEG Human Only",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Chimp Only",

  TRUE ~ "Other"
)

# Plot
ggplot(df_wide, aes(x = .data[[H_comp]], y = .data[[C_comp]], color = highlight)) +
  geom_point(size = 3, alpha = 0.8) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("T-DEG Human Only" = "red", "T-DEG Chimp Only" = "blue", "T-DEG Both" = "purple", "Other" = "grey70")) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, linetype = "dashed", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  annotate(
    "text",
    x = min(df_wide[[H_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    y = max(df_wide[[C_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    label = paste0(
      "R² = ", round(r2, 3),
      "\np = ", format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
    ),
    hjust = 0,
    vjust = 1
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(xlim = x_limits, ylim = y_limits) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = H_comp,
    y = C_comp,
    title = paste0(H_comp, " vs ", C_comp),
    color = "Gene Set"
  )

df_wide <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(H_comp, C_comp)) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  group_by(Gene, Comparisons) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = Comparisons, values_from = logFC) %>%
  filter(!is.na(.data[[H_comp]]), !is.na(.data[[C_comp]]))
